<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">рас-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ras-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пласта́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">plastátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***расплатиться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:расплатиться.html>расплати́ться</a> (7372)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">рас-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ras-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:платить.html>плати́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">platítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:расплатиться.html>расплати́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rasplatítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:расплачиваться.html>распла́чиваться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to pay off, to settle accounts with <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + intrumental</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>

***расплываться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:расплываться.html>расплыва́ться</a> (10391)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:расплыться.html>расплы́ться</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rasplýtʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ва́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-vátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:расплываться.html>расплыва́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rasplyvátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:расплыться.html>расплы́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to run
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чернила.html>черни́ла</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:расплываться.html>расплыва́ются</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:этот.html>э́той</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бумага.html>бума́ге</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">černíla <b>rasplyvájutsja</b> na étoj bumáge</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the ink runs on this paper</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to be blurred, to become fuzzy
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:слеза.html>слёз</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всё</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:расплываться.html>расплыва́лось</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>неё</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:перед.html>пе́ред</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глаз.html>глаза́ми</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ot sljóz vsjó <b>rasplyválosʹ</b> u nejó pered glazámi</i> ― <span class="e-translation">tears blurred her vision</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to run to fat, to grow obese</li>
<li>to sail away <i>(from one another)</i></li>
<li>to spread
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:расплываться.html>расплыва́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:улыбка.html>улы́бке</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>rasplyvátʹsja</b> v ulýbke</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to break into a smile</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:расплывчатый.html>расплы́вчатый</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">rasplývčatyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:плыть.html>плыть</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">plytʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поплыть.html>поплы́ть</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">poplýtʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:плавать.html>пла́вать</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">plávatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:плавание.html>пла́вание</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">plávanije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

***расплывчатый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:расплывчатый.html>расплы́вчатый</a> (13520)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">расплыв(а́ться)</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rasplyv(átʹsja)</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-чатый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-čatyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:расплывчатый.html>расплы́вчатый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rasplývčatyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>blurred, indistinct, fuzzy
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:расплывчатый.html>расплы́вчатое</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:изображение.html>изображе́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>rasplývčatoje</b> izobražénije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">blurred/fuzzy image</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>vague, indistinct
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:расплывчатый.html>расплы́вчатая</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:формулировка.html>формулиро́вка</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>rasplývčataja</b> formuliróvka</i> ― <span class="e-translation">vague/ambiguous wording</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***расплыться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:расплыться.html>расплы́ться</a> (9722)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">рас-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ras-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:плыть.html>плыть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">plytʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:расплыться.html>расплы́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rasplýtʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:расплываться.html>расплыва́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to run</li>
<li>to be blurred, to become fuzzy</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to run to fat, to grow obese</li>
<li>to sail away <i>(from one another)</i></li>
<li>to spread
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лицо.html>лицо́</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:расплывшийся.html>расплы́вшееся</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:улыбка.html>улы́бке</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">licó, rasplyvšejesja v ulýbke</i> ― <span class="e-translation">a face wreathed in a smile</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:плыть.html>плыть</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">plytʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поплыть.html>поплы́ть</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">poplýtʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

***распознать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:распознать.html>распозна́ть</a> (14110)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">рас-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ras-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:познать.html>позна́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">poznátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:распознать.html>распозна́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">raspoznátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:распознавать.html>распознава́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to recognize, to discern
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:распознать.html>распозна́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:болезнь.html>боле́знь</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>raspoznátʹ</b> boléznʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to diagnose the illness</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***располагать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:располагать.html>располага́ть</a> (4778)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">рас-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ras-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-лага́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-lagátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:располагать.html>располага́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">raspolagátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:расположить.html>расположи́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to dispose, to have available
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:человек.html>челове́к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:предполагать.html>предполага́ет</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>а</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бог.html>бог</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:располагать.html>располага́ет</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">čelovék predpolagájet, a box <b>raspolagájet</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">man proposes, God <b>disposes</b></span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to place, to dispose, to arrange, to set</li>
<li>to gain, to win over
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:расположить.html>расположи́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:себя.html>себе́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">raspoložítʹ k sebé</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to win favour</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to dispose, to be favourable, to be conducive</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:располагаться.html>располага́ться</a> (3703)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:располагать.html>располага́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">raspolagátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:располагаться.html>располага́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">raspolagátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">расположи́ться</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to settle oneself, to make oneself comfortable</li>
<li>to camp, to set up a camp, to take up a position</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:располагать.html>располага́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">raspolagátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***расползаться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:расползаться.html>располза́ться</a> (10851)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:расползтись.html>расползти́сь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">raspolztísʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:расползаться.html>располза́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">raspolzátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:расползтись.html>расползти́сь</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to crawl away</li>
<li>to spread, to run, to blur</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to spread, to sprawl
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:город.html>го́род</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:расползаться.html>располза́лся</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:вширь.html>вширь</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">górod <b>raspolzálsja</b> vširʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the town was sprawling</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to tear <i>(apart)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:расползаться.html>располза́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:шов.html>шва́м</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>raspolzátʹsja</b> po švam</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to tear/give at the seams</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to run to fat, to grow obese</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ползти.html>ползти́</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">polztí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поползти.html>поползти́</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">popolztí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">рас-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ras-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ползти.html>ползти́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">polztí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-сь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to tear <i>(apart)</i></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to run to fat, to grow obese</li></ol>

</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:расположение.html>расположе́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">raspoložénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:расположение.html>расположе́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:расположение.html>расположе́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:расположение.html>расположе́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>placement, arrangement, placing</li>
<li>situation, location, disposition</li>
<li>favour, liking</li>
<li>inclination (to, for); disposition (to, for), propensity</li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:расположить.html>располо́женный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">raspolóžennyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">past passive perfective participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:расположить.html>расположи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">raspoložítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span>: situated, located

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:расположить.html>располо́женный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">raspolóžennyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>disposed (towards, to)</li>
<li>inclined (to)</li></ol>

***расположить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:расположить.html>расположи́ть</a> (2091)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">рас-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ras-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:положить.html>положи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">položítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:расположить.html>расположи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">raspoložítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:располагать.html>располага́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to place, to dispose, to arrange, to set</li>
<li>to gain, to win over
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:расположить.html>расположи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:себя.html>себе́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>raspoložítʹ</b> k sebé</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to win favour</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to dispose, to be favourable, to be conducive</li></ol>

<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:располагаться.html>располага́ться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">raspolagátʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">расположи́ться</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">raspoložítʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:расположение.html>расположе́ние</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">raspoložénije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">рас-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ras-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пороть.html>поро́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">porótʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:распороть.html>распоро́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rasporótʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пороть.html>поро́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">распа́рывать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to unstitch, to tear at the seams
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfectives:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пороть.html>поро́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">porótʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">распа́рывать</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">raspáryvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to rip open (skin, a body part, etc.) with a sharp object
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">распа́рывать</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">raspáryvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">only</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>
